***разбор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбор.html>разбо́р</a> (9039)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбор.html>разбо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбор.html>разбо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбор.html>разбо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбор.html>разбо́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>analysis, review, critique, investigation, examination, inquiry
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбор.html>разбо́р</a> полёта</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razbór poljóta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">debriefing</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> parsing</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> trial, hearing</li>
<li>selectivity
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбор.html>разбо́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bez razbóra</i> ― <span class="e-translation">indiscriminately, without distinction</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбор.html>разбо́ром</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s razbórom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">discriminatingly, choosy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбор.html>разбо́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vse bez razbóra</i> ― <span class="e-translation">each and all</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***разборка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разборка.html>разбо́рка</a> (8114)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разобрать.html>разобра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razobrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, based on the nominal combining stem <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">разбор-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razbor-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, derived from the present tense stem <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">разбер-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razber-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with Indo-European <i>o</i>-vocalization characteristic of deverbal nouns.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разборка.html>разбо́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbórka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разборка.html>разбо́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разборка.html>разбо́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разборка.html>разбо́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sorting out</li>
<li>disassembling, dismantling, taking apart</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> showdown
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:криминальный.html>кримина́льная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разборка.html>разбо́рка</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kriminálʹnaja <b>razbórka</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">shoot-out</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***разборчивый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разборчивый.html>разбо́рчивый</a> (27833)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбор.html>разбо́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razbór</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-чивый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-čivyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разборчивый.html>разбо́рчивый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbórčivyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>legible, readable</li>
<li>scrupulous, fastidious</li>
<li>particular, choosy</li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбредаться.html>разбреда́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbredátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбрестись.html>разбрести́сь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wander off in different directions <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of many people</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брести.html>брести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбрестись.html>разбрести́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbrestísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбредаться.html>разбреда́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wander off in different directions <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of many people</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разброс.html>разбро́с</a> (31798)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбросать.html>разброса́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razbrosátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разброс.html>разбро́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbrós</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разброс.html>разбро́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разброс.html>разбро́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разброс.html>разбро́сов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dispersion, spread
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разброс.html>разбро́с</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:напряжение.html>напряже́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:измеренный.html>изме́ренного</a> им <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значительный.html>значи́телен</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Razbrós</b> značénij naprjažénija izmérennovo im byl značítelen.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Voltage values that he measured differed significantly.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбрызгивать.html>разбры́згивавший</a> (21550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбрызгивать.html>разбры́згивавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbrýzgivavšij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбрызгивать.html>разбры́згивать</a> (21550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбрызгивать.html>разбры́згивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbrýzgivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разбры́згать</b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбудить.html>разбуди́ть</a> (2520)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:будить.html>буди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">budítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухнуть.html>бу́хнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">búxnutʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to swell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<li>to grow excessively/immoderately, to inflate

***разбушеваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбушеваться.html>разбушева́ться</a> (26784)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бушевать.html>бушева́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">buševátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбушеваться.html>разбушева́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbuševátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to start to rage <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">harder and harder</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to go wild <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a storm, a drunk person, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>развёрнутый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvjórnutyj</span>)

<ol><li>extensive, large-scale, full-scale, all-out</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> deployed

***развал.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:развал.html>разва́л</a> (9994)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развал.html>разва́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развал.html>разва́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развал.html>разва́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развал.html>разва́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>disintegration, breakdown</li>
<li>disorganization, disorder</li>
<li>open-air bazaar
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:книжный.html>кни́жные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:развал.html>разва́лы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">knížnyje razvály</i> ― <span class="e-translation">bookstalls</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(wheel)</i> camber</li></ol>

***разваливаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разваливаться.html>разва́ливаться</a> (15244)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">разва́ливать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razválivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разваливаться.html>разва́ливаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razválivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развалиться.html>развали́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tumble down, to collapse</li>
<li>to go/fall to pieces, to break down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sprawl, to lounge</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">разва́ливать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razválivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">valítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развалить.html>развали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvalítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разва́ливать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pull down</li>
<li>to disorganize, to mess up</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:развалиться.html>развали́ться</a> (6067)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развалить.html>развали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развалиться.html>развали́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvalítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разваливаться.html>разва́ливаться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tumble down, to collapse</li>
<li>to go/fall to pieces, to break down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:развалиться.html>развали́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́лу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne datʹ <b>razvalítʹsja</b> délu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hold things together</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sprawl, to lounge</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развалить.html>развали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***разве.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разве.html>ра́зве</a> (428)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">развѣ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvě</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">only, besides</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the native <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">розвѣ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rozvě</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> was discontinued.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разве.html>ра́зве</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rázve</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>really
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разве.html>ра́зве</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:защитить.html>защити́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:диссертация.html>диссерта́цию</a>? <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разве.html>ра́зве</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́ет</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Rázve</b> ty ješčó ne zaščitíl dissertáciju? <b>Rázve</b> takóje byvájet?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Have you <b>really</b> not yet defended your thesis? Is this <b>really</b> the case?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">— <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a>. — <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разве.html>ра́зве</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— On tam byl. — <b>Rázve</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">"He was there." "Really?"</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> perhaps <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">often used in rhetorical questions</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разве.html>ра́зве</a></b> кто́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́ст</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взаймы.html>взаймы́</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Rázve</b> któ-libo dast vzajmý?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Perhaps</b> someone will give me a loan?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разве.html>ра́зве</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ешь</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Rázve</b> ty ne znáješʹ?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Don't you know?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разве.html>ра́зве</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:считать.html>счита́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>конца́</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Rázve</b> núžno jemú sčitátʹ s koncá?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Do you think he should count from the end?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> only</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unless
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:непременно.html>непреме́нно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лаю</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разве.html>ра́зве</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заболеть.html>заболе́ю</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja nepreménno éto sdélaju, <b>rázve</b> zaboléju.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I will certainly do it unless I get sick.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разве.html>ра́зве</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разве.html>ра́зве</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rázve</b> što, <b>rázve</b> tólʹko</i> ― <span class="e-translation">except perhaps</span></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кино.html>кино́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотрю́</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разве.html>ра́зве</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:комедия.html>коме́дии</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kinó ja ne smotrjú, <b>rázve što</b> komédii.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I don't watch any films except comedies, maybe.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неужели.html>неуже́ли</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neužéli</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>пра́вда</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">právda li</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
